2025-08-18T17:28:43.6026443Z         # StreamReader uses a future to link the protocol feed_data() method
2025-08-18T17:28:43.6026900Z         # to a read coroutine. Running two read coroutines at the same time
2025-08-18T17:28:43.6027339Z         # would have an unexpected behaviour. It would not possible to know
2025-08-18T17:28:43.6027720Z         # which coroutine would get the next data.

2025-08-18T17:28:43.6028410Z             raise RuntimeError(
2025-08-18T17:28:43.6028727Z                 f'{func_name}() called while another coroutine is '

2025-08-18T17:28:43.6029829Z     
2025-08-18T17:28:43.6030122Z         # Waiting for data while paused will make deadlock, so prevent it.
2025-08-18T17:28:43.6030579Z         # This is essential for readexactly(n) for case when n > self._limit.
